e\+A\+WT \mbox{\hyperlink{org_8citationstyles_8styles_8txt_a3faeb558038c811e203a436d48d23fc3}{and}} e\+IO A\+P\+Is \mbox{\hyperlink{org_8citationstyles_8styles_8txt_ab823061043c5cc565ab7bfa882774562}{for}} Java \mbox{\hyperlink{de_8undercouch_8citeproc-java_8txt_a99e0c7c6bd1082fe4cf97f0912e847d7}{on}} Mac OS X The \mbox{\hyperlink{org_8citationstyles_8styles_8txt_ab823061043c5cc565ab7bfa882774562}{for}} compilation \mbox{\hyperlink{org_8citationstyles_8styles_8txt_af796eca1ee2c70f9dd3321aadcf20bfe}{of}} \mbox{\hyperlink{de_8undercouch_8citeproc-java_8txt_a99101f1111e3615a81e34012de5a239b}{code}} \mbox{\hyperlink{de_8undercouch_8citeproc-java_8txt_a99e0c7c6bd1082fe4cf97f0912e847d7}{on}} platforms other than Mac OS X The jar \mbox{\hyperlink{de_8undercouch_8citeproc-java_8txt_a54c3aaa43358b77e4f57f4f72cbe56c6}{file}} is enclosed \mbox{\hyperlink{org_8citationstyles_8styles_8txt_a0297d2e7bc1126f2808896e7c19c7310}{in}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_readme_8txt_a4a72c9f4aeead17626fb9869ba1e4f1f}{a}} zip archive other platforms These stubs are not intended \mbox{\hyperlink{org_8citationstyles_8styles_8txt_ab823061043c5cc565ab7bfa882774562}{for}}
